           <dt>kha 3</dt>

           <dt>khalu </dt>
           <dd><em>kh&#x00e1;lu</em> ind. (as a particle of asseveration) indeed, verily, certainly, truly <a href="worksAuthorsAbbrs.html#R">R.</a> <a href="worksAuthorsAbbrs.html#&#x015a;ak">&#x015a;ak.</a> &amp;c </dd>
           <dd>&#x2022; (as a continuative particle) now, now then, now further <a href="worksAuthorsAbbrs.html#RV">RV.</a> x, 34, 14 <a href="worksAuthorsAbbrs.html#TS">TS.</a> &amp;c. ; (as a particle in syllogistic speech) but now, = Lat. <em>atqui</em> <a href="worksAuthorsAbbrs.html#TBr">TBr.</a> <a href="worksAuthorsAbbrs.html#&#x015a;Br">&#x015a;Br.</a> &amp;c </dd>
           <dd>&#x2022; [<em>khalu</em> is only exceptionally found at the beginning of a phrase </dd>
           <dd>&#x2022; it is frequently combined with other particles, thus <em>&#x00e1;tha kh&#x25cb;</em>, <em>u kh&#x25cb;</em>, <em>va&#x00ed; kh&#x25cb;</em>, <em>kh"&#x1e63; va&#x00ed;</em>, = now then, now further <a href="worksAuthorsAbbrs.html#TS">TS.</a> <a href="worksAuthorsAbbrs.html#TBr">TBr.</a> <a href="worksAuthorsAbbrs.html#&#x015a;Br">&#x015a;Br.</a> &amp;c </dd>
           <dd>&#x2022; in later Sansk&#x1e5b;it <em>khalu</em> frequently does little more than lay stress on the word by which it is preceded, and is sometimes merely expletive </dd>
           <dd>&#x2022; it is also a particle of prohibition (in which case it may be joined with the ind. p. [<em>khalu k&#x1e5b;tv&#x0101;</em>, 'desist from doing that'] <a href="worksAuthorsAbbrs.html#Nir">Nir.</a> i, 5 [also <em>&#x25cb;tam</em>] <a href="worksAuthorsAbbrs.html#P&#x0101;&#x1e47;">P&#x0101;&#x1e47;.</a> 3-4, 18 <a href="worksAuthorsAbbrs.html#&#x015a;i&#x015b;">&#x015a;i&#x015b;.</a> ii, 70) </dd>
           <dd>&#x2022; or of endearment, conciliation, and inquiry <a href="worksAuthorsAbbrs.html#L">L.</a> </dd>
           <dd>&#x2022; <em>na khalu</em>, by no means, not at all, indeed not <a href="worksAuthorsAbbrs.html#R">R.</a> &amp;c.]</dd>
